msg:It was my first time to travel to Chongzuo. When I searched for hotels on Ctrip before the trip, I was surprised to find that there is a five-star hotel in Chongzuo - Kaixuan International Hotel. But I booked a room with a river view because it was a five-star hotel. After checking in, I was delighted to find that this hotel is really good. It is a veritable five-star hotel with good value for money. The hotel facilities and equipment are very new, and the room decoration is very fine. The bathroom equipment that I am most concerned about is very easy to use. The faucet is easy to use and hot water comes out as soon as it is turned on. The shower is easy to use and the hot water is also very strong. The room is very clean, and the sheets, quilt covers, and bath towels are all very clean and comfortable. The most worthy of praise is that the hotel service level is very good. The service staff at the front desk are very enthusiastic, with a positive and friendly attitude. They enthusiastically introduced the various facilities of the hotel, and especially reminded that there is a self-service washing machine on the fifth floor that can be used for free. Although we didn't have time to use it, this should be a very friendly service content for tourists. As soon as we entered the room, we saw the riverside scenery outside the window under the sunset, which was very beautiful and photogenic.
